<div style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;"><b>Item 2.02 Results of Operations and Financial Condition</b></div>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -9pt;">&#xa0;</div>

<div style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;">On March 28, 2023, ParkerVision, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release which reported financial and operating results for the year ended December 31, 2022. A copy of the press release is attached as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference.</div>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -9pt;">&#xa0;</div>

<div style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;">The information contained in this Current Report on Form 8-K, including Exhibit 99.1 hereto, has been &#8220;furnished&#8221; and shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section 18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, or otherwise subject to liability under that section. The information in this Current Report shall not be incorporated by reference into any filing or other document pursuant to the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such filing or document.</div>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -9pt;">&#xa0;</div>

<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: right; font-size: 11pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif;"><font style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 11pt;"><b>&nbsp;Exhibit 99.1</b></font></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: left; font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif;"><font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 14pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: center; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b>ParkerVision Reports <a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="328299" data-tblv="5" id="led328299F2023271678205059185">2022</a> Results</b></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b>JACKSONVILLE</b><b>, Fla.,&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="21x1" data-tblname="328299" data-tblv="5" id="led328299F2023271678205039778">March 28, 2023</a> </b>&#8211;<b> </b>ParkerVision, Inc. (OTCQB: PRKR) (&#8220;ParkerVision&#8221;), a developer and marketer of technologies and products for wireless applications, today announced results for the year ended <a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="328299" data-tblv="5" id="led328299F2023271678205050890">December 31, 2022</a>.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b><i>Year End&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="328299" data-tblv="5" id="led328299F2023271678205077734">2022</a> Summary and Recent Developments</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 34pt; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Through March 2023, the Company has resolved patent infringement actions filed in 2020 and 2021 in the Western District of Texas against four of six defendants through patent license and settlement agreements, including one agreement reached in the first quarter of 2023 for which the Company received $25 million in gross proceeds.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 34pt; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">New patent infringement cases were filed against MediaTek and Realtek in the Western District of Texas in the fourth quarter of 2022.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 81pt; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">o</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Pending cases against TCL and LG in Texas are stayed pending the outcome of one or both of the Realtek and MediaTek actions.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 34pt; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Hearing at the Federal Circuit for the Company's appeal in <i>ParkerVision v. Qualcomm</i> is expected to be held mid-2023.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 81pt; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">o</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">The appeal is the result of March 2022 Florida district court rulings in Qualcomm's favor on pre-trial motions that resulted in eliminating all matters for a jury to decide in an infringement case against Qualcomm that was nearing trial after being filed nearly nine years prior in 2014.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 34pt; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Sanford (Sandy) Litvack joined the ParkerVision board of directors in October 2022.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">Jeffrey Parker, Chairman and Chief Executive Officer, commented, &#8220;ParkerVision holds a portfolio of over 100 patents on our inventions, including a number of expired patents for which claims can be made for past damages, as well as a number of patents that will not expire for years to come.&nbsp; We believe our technologies are being used, without our permission, in a range of cellular, Wifi and Bluetooth chips and devices.&nbsp; Our patented technologies have all been developed in-house as a result of significant R&amp;D investments, and our team includes our lead inventors whose knowledge and experience provide a strong foundation for enforcing the property rights of our claims against companies who we believe are wrongly using our patented inventions."</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-variant:normal;text-align:center;margin:0pt;">&#65279;</p>

<div class="PGBK" style="width: 100%; margin-left: 0pt; margin-right: 0pt">
<div class="PGFTR" style="text-align: center; width: 100%">
<div class="hf-row">
<div class="hf-cell PGNUM">&nbsp;</div>
</div>
</div>

<hr style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; border: none; width: 100%; height: 2px; color: #000000; background-color: #000000">
<div class="PGHDR" style="text-align: left; width: 100%">
<div class="hf-row">
<div class="hf-cell TOCLink">&nbsp;</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">Mr. Parker continued, &#8220;We currently have patent enforcement cases pending against Qualcomm, Apple, TCL, LG, MediaTek and Realtek, and expect to file additional cases this year.&nbsp; We also have a patent enforcement action against Qualcomm, involving significant damages claims, on which we have filed an appeal at the Federal Circuit.&nbsp; We anticipate a hearing date for our appeal will be set for mid-2023.</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">"The incoming revenues from our overall patent enforcement program, after payment of contingent legal fees and expenses, will be used to reduce a significant portion of the Company's contingent debt.&nbsp; We expect 2023 to be a profitable year for ParkerVision."</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b><i>Financial Results</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

			<td style="width: 34pt; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Net loss for&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="328299" data-tblv="5" id="led328299F2023271678206231607">2022</a> was&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="328303" data-tblv="5" id="led328303F2023271678206310573">$9.8</a> million, or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="6x1" data-tblname="328303" data-tblv="5" id="led328303F2023271678209514132">$0.13</a> per common share, compared to a net loss of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x2" data-tblname="328303" data-tblv="5" id="led328303F2023271678206360495">$12.3</a> million, or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="6x2" data-tblname="328303" data-tblv="5" id="led328303F2023271678209525269">$0.17</a> per common share for <a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="328299" data-tblv="5" id="led328299F2023271678206410215">2021</a>.</p>
			</td>

<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>About ParkerVision</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt;">ParkerVision, Inc. invents, develops and licenses cutting-edge, proprietary radio-frequency (RF) technologies that enable wireless solution providers to make and sell advanced wireless communication products. &nbsp;ParkerVision is engaged in a number of patent enforcement actions in the U.S. to protect patented rights that it believes are broadly infringed by others. For more information, please visit www.parkervision.com.<i> (PRKR-I)</i></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>Safe Harbor Statement</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt;"><i>This press release contains forward-looking information. Readers are cautioned not to place undue reliance on any such forward-looking statements, each of which speaks only as of the date made. Such statements are subject to certain risks and uncertainties that are disclosed in the Company</i>&#8217;<i>s SEC reports, including the Form 10-K for the year ended <a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="328299" data-tblv="5" id="led328299F2023271678206602212">December 31, 2022</a></i><i>. These risks and uncertainties could cause actual results to differ materially from those currently anticipated or projected.</i></p>
